2020-07-20 16:11:27 => SELECT `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                            tblShopProductDetails.productDetails
                            SEPARATOR "!#$%="
                    ) AS productDetails, `tbl_shop_products`.`stock`, `tbl_shop_products`.`recommendedQuantity`, `tbl_shop_products`.`active` AS `productActive`, `tbl_shop_products`.`showImage`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` AS `dateTimeFrom`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` AS `dateTimeTo`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`category`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`id` AS `categoryId`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` AS `categoryActive`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                        CONCAT(
                            tbl_shop_printers.id, '#%!$%=?', `tbl_shop_printers`.`printer`, '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_printers.active
                        )
                    ) AS printers, `tblShopProductTimes`.`productTimes`, `tblShopAddons`.`addons` AS `addons`
FROM `tbl_shop_products_extended`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_products` ON `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_categories` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`categoryId` = `tbl_shop_categories`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_product_printers` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`id` = `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`productId`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_printers` ON `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`printerId` = `tbl_shop_printers`.`id`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT
                                tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_product_times.day,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_product_times.timeTo
                                    SEPARATOR "!#$%="
                                ) AS productTimes                                
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_product_times
                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_product_times.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom ASC
                        ) tblShopProductTimes ON `tblShopProductTimes`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
INNER JOIN `tbl_shop_products_types` ON `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productTypeId`
INNER JOIN (
                            SELECT tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.id,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.shortDescription,
                                    '#%!$%=?',FORMAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.price,2),
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.vatpercentage,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_products_types.type,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_products_types.isMain,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.updateCycle,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.showInPublic,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.productId,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_categories.category,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_products.active,
                                    '#%!$%=?', IF(CHAR_LENGTH(tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription) > 0, tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription, "")
                                    ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.id DESC
                                    SEPARATOR "!#$%="                                    
                                ) AS productDetails
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_extended
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products_types ON tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId = tbl_shop_products_types.id
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products.id = tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_categories ON tbl_shop_categories.id = tbl_shop_products.categoryId

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId DESC
                            
                        ) tblShopProductDetails ON `tblShopProductDetails`.`productTypeId` = `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` AND `tblShopProductDetails`.`name` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`name`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT 
                                tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_products_addons.addonProductId,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_products_addons.productExtendedId

                                    SEPARATOR "!#$%="                                    
                                ) AS addons
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_addons
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products_addons.productId = tbl_shop_products.id

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_addons.productId
                            
                        ) tblShopAddons ON `tblShopAddons`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
WHERE `tbl_shop_categories`.`userId` = 418
AND `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` = '1'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` <= '2020-07-20 16:11:27'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` > '2020-07-20 16:11:27'
GROUP BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
ORDER BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`id` DESC

INNER JOIN `tbl_user` ON `tbl_user`.`id` = `tbl_shop_vendors`.`vendorId`

2020-07-20 16:50:21 => SELECT `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                            tblShopProductDetails.productDetails
                            SEPARATOR "!#$%="
                    ) AS productDetails, `tbl_shop_products`.`stock`, `tbl_shop_products`.`recommendedQuantity`, `tbl_shop_products`.`active` AS `productActive`, `tbl_shop_products`.`showImage`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` AS `dateTimeFrom`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` AS `dateTimeTo`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`category`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`id` AS `categoryId`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` AS `categoryActive`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                        CONCAT(
                            tbl_shop_printers.id, '#%!$%=?', `tbl_shop_printers`.`printer`, '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_printers.active
                        )
                    ) AS printers, `tblShopProductTimes`.`productTimes`, `tblShopAddons`.`addons` AS `addons`
FROM `tbl_shop_products_extended`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_products` ON `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_categories` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`categoryId` = `tbl_shop_categories`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_product_printers` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`id` = `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`productId`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_printers` ON `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`printerId` = `tbl_shop_printers`.`id`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT
                                tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_product_times.day,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_product_times.timeTo
                                    SEPARATOR "!#$%="
                                ) AS productTimes                                
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_product_times
                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_product_times.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom ASC
                        ) tblShopProductTimes ON `tblShopProductTimes`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
INNER JOIN `tbl_shop_products_types` ON `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productTypeId`
INNER JOIN (
                            SELECT tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.id,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.shortDescription,
                                    '#%!$%=?',FORMAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.price,2),
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.vatpercentage,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_products_types.type,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_products_types.isMain,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.updateCycle,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.showInPublic,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.productId,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_categories.category,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_products.active,
                                    '#%!$%=?', IF(CHAR_LENGTH(tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription) > 0, tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription, "")
                                    ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.id DESC
                                    SEPARATOR "!#$%="                                    
                                ) AS productDetails
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_extended
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products_types ON tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId = tbl_shop_products_types.id
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products.id = tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_categories ON tbl_shop_categories.id = tbl_shop_products.categoryId

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId DESC
                            
                        ) tblShopProductDetails ON `tblShopProductDetails`.`productTypeId` = `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` AND `tblShopProductDetails`.`name` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`name`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT 
                                tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_products_addons.addonProductId,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_products_addons.productExtendedId

                                    SEPARATOR "!#$%="                                    
                                ) AS addons
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_addons
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products_addons.productId = tbl_shop_products.id

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_addons.productId
                            
                        ) tblShopAddons ON `tblShopAddons`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
WHERE `tbl_shop_categories`.`userId` = 418
AND `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` = '1'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` <= '2020-07-20 16:50:21'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` > '2020-07-20 16:50:21'
GROUP BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
ORDER BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`id` DESC

                    ) AS productDetails, `tbl_shop_products`.`stock`, `tbl_shop_products`.`recommendedQuantity`, `tbl_shop_products`.`active` AS `productActive`, `tbl_shop_products`.`showImage`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` AS `dateTimeFrom`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` AS `dateTimeTo`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`category`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`id` AS `categoryId`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` AS `categoryActive`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                        CONCAT(
                            tbl_shop_printers.id, '#%!$%=?', `tbl_shop_printers`.`printer`, '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_printers.active
                        )
                    ) AS printers, `tblShopProductTimes`.`productTimes`, `tblShopAddons`.`addons` AS `addons`
FROM `tbl_shop_products_extended`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_products` ON `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_categories` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`categoryId` = `tbl_shop_categories`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_product_printers` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`id` = `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`productId`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_printers` ON `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`printerId` = `tbl_shop_printers`.`id`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT
                                tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_product_times.day,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_product_times.timeTo
                                    SEPARATOR "!#$%="
                                ) AS productTimes                                
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_product_times
                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_product_times.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom ASC
                        ) tblShopProductTimes ON `tblShopProductTimes`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
INNER JOIN `tbl_shop_products_types` ON `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productTypeId`
INNER JOIN (

                                GROUP_CONCAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.id,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.shortDescription,
                                    '#%!$%=?',FORMAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.price,2),
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.vatpercentage,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_products_types.type,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_products_types.isMain,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.updateCycle,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.showInPublic,
                                    '#%!$%=?',tbl_shop_products_extended.productId,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_categories.category,
                                    '#%!$%=?', tbl_shop_products.active,
                                    '#%!$%=?', IF(CHAR_LENGTH(tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription) > 0, tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription, "")
                                    ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.id DESC
                                    SEPARATOR "!#$%="                                    
                                ) AS productDetails
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_extended
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products_types ON tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId = tbl_shop_products_types.id
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products.id = tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_categories ON tbl_shop_categories.id = tbl_shop_products.categoryId

                        ) tblShopAddons ON `tblShopAddons`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`

2020-07-27 15:51:41 => SELECT `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                            tblShopProductDetails.productDetails
                            SEPARATOR ")$="
                    ) AS productDetails, `tbl_shop_products`.`stock`, `tbl_shop_products`.`recommendedQuantity`, `tbl_shop_products`.`active` AS `productActive`, `tbl_shop_products`.`showImage`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` AS `dateTimeFrom`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` AS `dateTimeTo`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`category`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`id` AS `categoryId`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` AS `categoryActive`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber` AS `sortNumber`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                        CONCAT(
                            tbl_shop_printers.id, ')#%', `tbl_shop_printers`.`printer`, ')#%', tbl_shop_printers.active
                        )
                    ) AS printers, `tblShopProductTimes`.`productTimes`, `tblShopAddons`.`addons` AS `addons`
FROM `tbl_shop_products_extended`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_products` ON `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_categories` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`categoryId` = `tbl_shop_categories`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_product_printers` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`id` = `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`productId`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_printers` ON `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`printerId` = `tbl_shop_printers`.`id`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT
                                tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.day,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeTo
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="
                                ) AS productTimes                                
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_product_times
                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_product_times.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom ASC
                        ) tblShopProductTimes ON `tblShopProductTimes`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
INNER JOIN `tbl_shop_products_types` ON `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productTypeId`
INNER JOIN (
                            SELECT tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.id,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.shortDescription,
                                    ')#%',FORMAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.price,2),
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.vatpercentage,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.type,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.isMain,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.updateCycle,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.showInPublic,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_categories.category,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products.active,
                                    ')#%', IF(CHAR_LENGTH(tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription) > 0, tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription, "")
                                    ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.id DESC
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS productDetails
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_extended
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products_types ON tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId = tbl_shop_products_types.id
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products.id = tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_categories ON tbl_shop_categories.id = tbl_shop_products.categoryId

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId DESC
                            
                        ) tblShopProductDetails ON `tblShopProductDetails`.`productTypeId` = `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` AND `tblShopProductDetails`.`name` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`name`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT 
                                tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.addonProductId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.productExtendedId

                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS addons
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_addons
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products_addons.productId = tbl_shop_products.id

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_addons.productId
                            
                        ) tblShopAddons ON `tblShopAddons`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
WHERE `tbl_shop_categories`.`userId` = 1162
GROUP BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
ORDER BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`id` DESC

2020-07-27 15:53:09 => SELECT `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                            tblShopProductDetails.productDetails
                            SEPARATOR ")$="
                    ) AS productDetails, `tbl_shop_products`.`stock`, `tbl_shop_products`.`recommendedQuantity`, `tbl_shop_products`.`active` AS `productActive`, `tbl_shop_products`.`showImage`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` AS `dateTimeFrom`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` AS `dateTimeTo`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`category`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`id` AS `categoryId`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` AS `categoryActive`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber` AS `sortNumber`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                        CONCAT(
                            tbl_shop_printers.id, ')#%', `tbl_shop_printers`.`printer`, ')#%', tbl_shop_printers.active
                        )
                    ) AS printers, `tblShopProductTimes`.`productTimes`, `tblShopAddons`.`addons` AS `addons`
FROM `tbl_shop_products_extended`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_products` ON `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_categories` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`categoryId` = `tbl_shop_categories`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_product_printers` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`id` = `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`productId`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_printers` ON `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`printerId` = `tbl_shop_printers`.`id`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT
                                tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.day,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeTo
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="
                                ) AS productTimes                                
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_product_times
                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_product_times.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom ASC
                        ) tblShopProductTimes ON `tblShopProductTimes`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
INNER JOIN `tbl_shop_products_types` ON `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productTypeId`
INNER JOIN (
                            SELECT tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.id,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.shortDescription,
                                    ')#%',FORMAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.price,2),
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.vatpercentage,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.type,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.isMain,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.updateCycle,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.showInPublic,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_categories.category,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products.active,
                                    ')#%', IF(CHAR_LENGTH(tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription) > 0, tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription, "")
                                    ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.id DESC
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS productDetails
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_extended
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products_types ON tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId = tbl_shop_products_types.id
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products.id = tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_categories ON tbl_shop_categories.id = tbl_shop_products.categoryId

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId DESC
                            
                        ) tblShopProductDetails ON `tblShopProductDetails`.`productTypeId` = `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` AND `tblShopProductDetails`.`name` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`name`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT 
                                tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.addonProductId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.productExtendedId

                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS addons
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_addons
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products_addons.productId = tbl_shop_products.id

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_addons.productId
                            
                        ) tblShopAddons ON `tblShopAddons`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
WHERE `tbl_shop_categories`.`userId` = 1162
GROUP BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
ORDER BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`id` DESC

FROM `tbl_shop_spot_products`

2020-07-27 15:56:25 => SELECT `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                            tblShopProductDetails.productDetails
                            SEPARATOR ")$="
                    ) AS productDetails, `tbl_shop_products`.`stock`, `tbl_shop_products`.`recommendedQuantity`, `tbl_shop_products`.`active` AS `productActive`, `tbl_shop_products`.`showImage`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` AS `dateTimeFrom`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` AS `dateTimeTo`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`category`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`id` AS `categoryId`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` AS `categoryActive`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber` AS `sortNumber`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                        CONCAT(
                            tbl_shop_printers.id, ')#%', `tbl_shop_printers`.`printer`, ')#%', tbl_shop_printers.active
                        )
                    ) AS printers, `tblShopProductTimes`.`productTimes`, `tblShopAddons`.`addons` AS `addons`
FROM `tbl_shop_products_extended`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_products` ON `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_categories` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`categoryId` = `tbl_shop_categories`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_product_printers` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`id` = `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`productId`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_printers` ON `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`printerId` = `tbl_shop_printers`.`id`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT
                                tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.day,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeTo
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="
                                ) AS productTimes                                
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_product_times
                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_product_times.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom ASC
                        ) tblShopProductTimes ON `tblShopProductTimes`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
INNER JOIN `tbl_shop_products_types` ON `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productTypeId`
INNER JOIN (
                            SELECT tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.id,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.shortDescription,
                                    ')#%',FORMAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.price,2),
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.vatpercentage,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.type,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.isMain,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.updateCycle,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.showInPublic,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_categories.category,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products.active,
                                    ')#%', IF(CHAR_LENGTH(tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription) > 0, tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription, "")
                                    ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.id DESC
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS productDetails
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_extended
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products_types ON tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId = tbl_shop_products_types.id
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products.id = tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_categories ON tbl_shop_categories.id = tbl_shop_products.categoryId

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId DESC
                            
                        ) tblShopProductDetails ON `tblShopProductDetails`.`productTypeId` = `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` AND `tblShopProductDetails`.`name` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`name`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT 
                                tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.addonProductId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.productExtendedId

                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS addons
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_addons
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products_addons.productId = tbl_shop_products.id

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_addons.productId
                            
                        ) tblShopAddons ON `tblShopAddons`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
WHERE `tbl_shop_categories`.`userId` = 1162

2020-07-27 15:58:12 => SELECT `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                            tblShopProductDetails.productDetails
                            SEPARATOR ")$="
                    ) AS productDetails, `tbl_shop_products`.`stock`, `tbl_shop_products`.`recommendedQuantity`, `tbl_shop_products`.`active` AS `productActive`, `tbl_shop_products`.`showImage`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` AS `dateTimeFrom`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` AS `dateTimeTo`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`category`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`id` AS `categoryId`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` AS `categoryActive`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber` AS `sortNumber`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                        CONCAT(
                            tbl_shop_printers.id, ')#%', `tbl_shop_printers`.`printer`, ')#%', tbl_shop_printers.active
                        )
                    ) AS printers, `tblShopProductTimes`.`productTimes`, `tblShopAddons`.`addons` AS `addons`
FROM `tbl_shop_products_extended`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_products` ON `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_categories` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`categoryId` = `tbl_shop_categories`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_product_printers` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`id` = `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`productId`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_printers` ON `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`printerId` = `tbl_shop_printers`.`id`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT
                                tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.day,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeTo
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="
                                ) AS productTimes                                
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_product_times
                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_product_times.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom ASC
                        ) tblShopProductTimes ON `tblShopProductTimes`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
INNER JOIN `tbl_shop_products_types` ON `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productTypeId`
INNER JOIN (
                            SELECT tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.id,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.shortDescription,
                                    ')#%',FORMAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.price,2),
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.vatpercentage,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.type,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.isMain,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.updateCycle,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.showInPublic,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_categories.category,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products.active,
                                    ')#%', IF(CHAR_LENGTH(tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription) > 0, tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription, "")
                                    ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.id DESC
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS productDetails
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_extended
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products_types ON tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId = tbl_shop_products_types.id
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products.id = tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_categories ON tbl_shop_categories.id = tbl_shop_products.categoryId

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId DESC
                            
                        ) tblShopProductDetails ON `tblShopProductDetails`.`productTypeId` = `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` AND `tblShopProductDetails`.`name` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`name`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT 
                                tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.addonProductId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.productExtendedId

                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS addons
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_addons
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products_addons.productId = tbl_shop_products.id

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_addons.productId
                            
                        ) tblShopAddons ON `tblShopAddons`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
WHERE `tbl_shop_categories`.`userId` = 1162
AND `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` = '1'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` <= '2020-07-27 15:58:11'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` > '2020-07-27 15:58:11'
GROUP BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
ORDER BY `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber`

2020-07-27 15:59:30 => SELECT `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                            tblShopProductDetails.productDetails
                            SEPARATOR ")$="
                    ) AS productDetails, `tbl_shop_products`.`stock`, `tbl_shop_products`.`recommendedQuantity`, `tbl_shop_products`.`active` AS `productActive`, `tbl_shop_products`.`showImage`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` AS `dateTimeFrom`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` AS `dateTimeTo`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`category`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`id` AS `categoryId`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` AS `categoryActive`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber` AS `sortNumber`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                        CONCAT(
                            tbl_shop_printers.id, ')#%', `tbl_shop_printers`.`printer`, ')#%', tbl_shop_printers.active
                        )
                    ) AS printers, `tblShopProductTimes`.`productTimes`, `tblShopAddons`.`addons` AS `addons`
FROM `tbl_shop_products_extended`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_products` ON `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_categories` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`categoryId` = `tbl_shop_categories`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_product_printers` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`id` = `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`productId`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_printers` ON `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`printerId` = `tbl_shop_printers`.`id`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT
                                tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.day,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeTo
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="
                                ) AS productTimes                                
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_product_times
                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_product_times.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom ASC
                        ) tblShopProductTimes ON `tblShopProductTimes`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
INNER JOIN `tbl_shop_products_types` ON `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productTypeId`
INNER JOIN (
                            SELECT tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.id,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.shortDescription,
                                    ')#%',FORMAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.price,2),
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.vatpercentage,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.type,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.isMain,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.updateCycle,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.showInPublic,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_categories.category,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products.active,
                                    ')#%', IF(CHAR_LENGTH(tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription) > 0, tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription, "")
                                    ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.id DESC
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS productDetails
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_extended
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products_types ON tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId = tbl_shop_products_types.id
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products.id = tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_categories ON tbl_shop_categories.id = tbl_shop_products.categoryId

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId DESC
                            
                        ) tblShopProductDetails ON `tblShopProductDetails`.`productTypeId` = `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` AND `tblShopProductDetails`.`name` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`name`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT 
                                tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.addonProductId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.productExtendedId

                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS addons
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_addons
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products_addons.productId = tbl_shop_products.id

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_addons.productId
                            
                        ) tblShopAddons ON `tblShopAddons`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
WHERE `tbl_shop_categories`.`userId` = 1162
AND `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` = '1'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` <= '2020-07-27 15:59:29'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` > '2020-07-27 15:59:29'
GROUP BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
ORDER BY `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber`

                    ) AS printers, `tblShopProductTimes`.`productTimes`, `tblShopAddons`.`addons` AS `addons`
FROM `tbl_shop_products_extended`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_products` ON `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_categories` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`categoryId` = `tbl_shop_categories`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_product_printers` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`id` = `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`productId`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_printers` ON `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`printerId` = `tbl_shop_printers`.`id`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT
                                tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.day,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeTo
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="
                                ) AS productTimes                                
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_product_times
                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_product_times.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom ASC
                        ) tblShopProductTimes ON `tblShopProductTimes`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
INNER JOIN `tbl_shop_products_types` ON `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productTypeId`
INNER JOIN (
                            SELECT tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.id,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.shortDescription,
                                    ')#%',FORMAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.price,2),
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.vatpercentage,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.type,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.isMain,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.updateCycle,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.showInPublic,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_categories.category,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products.active,
                                    ')#%', IF(CHAR_LENGTH(tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription) > 0, tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription, "")
                                    ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.id DESC
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS productDetails
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_extended
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products_types ON tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId = tbl_shop_products_types.id
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products.id = tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_categories ON tbl_shop_categories.id = tbl_shop_products.categoryId

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId DESC
                            
                        ) tblShopProductDetails ON `tblShopProductDetails`.`productTypeId` = `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` AND `tblShopProductDetails`.`name` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`name`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT 
                                tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.addonProductId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.productExtendedId

                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS addons
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_addons
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products_addons.productId = tbl_shop_products.id

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_addons.productId
                            
                        ) tblShopAddons ON `tblShopAddons`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
WHERE `tbl_shop_categories`.`userId` = 1162
AND `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` = '1'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` <= '2020-07-27 16:06:33'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` > '2020-07-27 16:06:33'
GROUP BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
ORDER BY `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber`

2020-07-27 16:07:07 => SELECT `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                            tblShopProductDetails.productDetails
                            SEPARATOR ")$="
                    ) AS productDetails, `tbl_shop_products`.`stock`, `tbl_shop_products`.`recommendedQuantity`, `tbl_shop_products`.`active` AS `productActive`, `tbl_shop_products`.`showImage`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` AS `dateTimeFrom`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` AS `dateTimeTo`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`category`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`id` AS `categoryId`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` AS `categoryActive`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber` AS `sortNumber`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                        CONCAT(
                            tbl_shop_printers.id, ')#%', `tbl_shop_printers`.`printer`, ')#%', tbl_shop_printers.active
                        )
                    ) AS printers, `tblShopProductTimes`.`productTimes`, `tblShopAddons`.`addons` AS `addons`
FROM `tbl_shop_products_extended`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_products` ON `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_categories` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`categoryId` = `tbl_shop_categories`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_product_printers` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`id` = `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`productId`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_printers` ON `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`printerId` = `tbl_shop_printers`.`id`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT
                                tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.day,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeTo
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="
                                ) AS productTimes                                
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_product_times
                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_product_times.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom ASC
                        ) tblShopProductTimes ON `tblShopProductTimes`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
INNER JOIN `tbl_shop_products_types` ON `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productTypeId`
INNER JOIN (
                            SELECT tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.id,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.shortDescription,
                                    ')#%',FORMAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.price,2),
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.vatpercentage,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.type,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.isMain,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.updateCycle,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.showInPublic,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_categories.category,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products.active,
                                    ')#%', IF(CHAR_LENGTH(tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription) > 0, tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription, "")
                                    ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.id DESC
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS productDetails
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_extended
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products_types ON tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId = tbl_shop_products_types.id
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products.id = tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_categories ON tbl_shop_categories.id = tbl_shop_products.categoryId

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId DESC
                            
                        ) tblShopProductDetails ON `tblShopProductDetails`.`productTypeId` = `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` AND `tblShopProductDetails`.`name` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`name`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT 
                                tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.addonProductId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.productExtendedId

                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS addons
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_addons
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products_addons.productId = tbl_shop_products.id

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_addons.productId
                            
                        ) tblShopAddons ON `tblShopAddons`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
WHERE `tbl_shop_categories`.`userId` = 1162
AND `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` = '1'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` <= '2020-07-27 16:07:07'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` > '2020-07-27 16:07:07'
GROUP BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
ORDER BY `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber`

2020-07-27 16:10:25 => SELECT `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                            tblShopProductDetails.productDetails
                            SEPARATOR ")$="
                    ) AS productDetails, `tbl_shop_products`.`stock`, `tbl_shop_products`.`recommendedQuantity`, `tbl_shop_products`.`active` AS `productActive`, `tbl_shop_products`.`showImage`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` AS `dateTimeFrom`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` AS `dateTimeTo`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`category`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`id` AS `categoryId`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` AS `categoryActive`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber` AS `sortNumber`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                        CONCAT(
                            tbl_shop_printers.id, ')#%', `tbl_shop_printers`.`printer`, ')#%', tbl_shop_printers.active
                        )
                    ) AS printers, `tblShopProductTimes`.`productTimes`, `tblShopAddons`.`addons` AS `addons`
FROM `tbl_shop_products_extended`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_products` ON `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_categories` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`categoryId` = `tbl_shop_categories`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_product_printers` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`id` = `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`productId`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_printers` ON `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`printerId` = `tbl_shop_printers`.`id`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT
                                tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.day,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeTo
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="
                                ) AS productTimes                                
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_product_times
                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_product_times.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom ASC
                        ) tblShopProductTimes ON `tblShopProductTimes`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
INNER JOIN `tbl_shop_products_types` ON `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productTypeId`
INNER JOIN (
                            SELECT tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.id,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.shortDescription,
                                    ')#%',FORMAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.price,2),
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.vatpercentage,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.type,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.isMain,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.updateCycle,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.showInPublic,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_categories.category,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products.active,
                                    ')#%', IF(CHAR_LENGTH(tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription) > 0, tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription, "")
                                    ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.id DESC
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS productDetails
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_extended
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products_types ON tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId = tbl_shop_products_types.id
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products.id = tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_categories ON tbl_shop_categories.id = tbl_shop_products.categoryId

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId DESC
                            
                        ) tblShopProductDetails ON `tblShopProductDetails`.`productTypeId` = `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` AND `tblShopProductDetails`.`name` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`name`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT 
                                tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.addonProductId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.productExtendedId

                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS addons
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_addons
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products_addons.productId = tbl_shop_products.id

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_addons.productId
                            
                        ) tblShopAddons ON `tblShopAddons`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
WHERE `tbl_shop_categories`.`userId` = 1162
AND `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` = '1'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` <= '2020-07-27 16:10:25'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` > '2020-07-27 16:10:25'
GROUP BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
ORDER BY `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber`

2020-07-27 16:10:38 => SELECT `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                            tblShopProductDetails.productDetails
                            SEPARATOR ")$="
                    ) AS productDetails, `tbl_shop_products`.`stock`, `tbl_shop_products`.`recommendedQuantity`, `tbl_shop_products`.`active` AS `productActive`, `tbl_shop_products`.`showImage`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` AS `dateTimeFrom`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` AS `dateTimeTo`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`category`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`id` AS `categoryId`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` AS `categoryActive`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber` AS `sortNumber`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                        CONCAT(
                            tbl_shop_printers.id, ')#%', `tbl_shop_printers`.`printer`, ')#%', tbl_shop_printers.active
                        )
                    ) AS printers, `tblShopProductTimes`.`productTimes`, `tblShopAddons`.`addons` AS `addons`
FROM `tbl_shop_products_extended`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_products` ON `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_categories` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`categoryId` = `tbl_shop_categories`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_product_printers` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`id` = `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`productId`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_printers` ON `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`printerId` = `tbl_shop_printers`.`id`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT
                                tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.day,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeTo
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="
                                ) AS productTimes                                
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_product_times
                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_product_times.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom ASC
                        ) tblShopProductTimes ON `tblShopProductTimes`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
INNER JOIN `tbl_shop_products_types` ON `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productTypeId`
INNER JOIN (
                            SELECT tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.id,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.shortDescription,
                                    ')#%',FORMAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.price,2),
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.vatpercentage,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.type,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.isMain,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.updateCycle,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.showInPublic,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_categories.category,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products.active,
                                    ')#%', IF(CHAR_LENGTH(tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription) > 0, tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription, "")
                                    ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.id DESC
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS productDetails
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_extended
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products_types ON tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId = tbl_shop_products_types.id
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products.id = tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_categories ON tbl_shop_categories.id = tbl_shop_products.categoryId

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId DESC
                            
                        ) tblShopProductDetails ON `tblShopProductDetails`.`productTypeId` = `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` AND `tblShopProductDetails`.`name` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`name`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT 
                                tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.addonProductId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.productExtendedId

                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS addons
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_addons
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products_addons.productId = tbl_shop_products.id

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_addons.productId
                            
                        ) tblShopAddons ON `tblShopAddons`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
WHERE `tbl_shop_categories`.`userId` = 1162
AND `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` = '1'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` <= '2020-07-27 16:10:37'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` > '2020-07-27 16:10:37'
GROUP BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
ORDER BY `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber`

2020-07-27 16:11:00 => SELECT `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                            tblShopProductDetails.productDetails
                            SEPARATOR ")$="
                    ) AS productDetails, `tbl_shop_products`.`stock`, `tbl_shop_products`.`recommendedQuantity`, `tbl_shop_products`.`active` AS `productActive`, `tbl_shop_products`.`showImage`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` AS `dateTimeFrom`, `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` AS `dateTimeTo`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`category`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`id` AS `categoryId`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` AS `categoryActive`, `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber` AS `sortNumber`, GROUP_CONCAT(
                        CONCAT(
                            tbl_shop_printers.id, ')#%', `tbl_shop_printers`.`printer`, ')#%', tbl_shop_printers.active
                        )
                    ) AS printers, `tblShopProductTimes`.`productTimes`, `tblShopAddons`.`addons` AS `addons`
FROM `tbl_shop_products_extended`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_products` ON `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_categories` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`categoryId` = `tbl_shop_categories`.`id`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_product_printers` ON `tbl_shop_products`.`id` = `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`productId`
LEFT JOIN `tbl_shop_printers` ON `tbl_shop_product_printers`.`printerId` = `tbl_shop_printers`.`id`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT
                                tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_product_times.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.day,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_product_times.timeTo
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="
                                ) AS productTimes                                
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_product_times
                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_product_times.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_product_times.timeFrom ASC
                        ) tblShopProductTimes ON `tblShopProductTimes`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
INNER JOIN `tbl_shop_products_types` ON `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productTypeId`
INNER JOIN (
                            SELECT tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.id,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.name,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.shortDescription,
                                    ')#%',FORMAT(tbl_shop_products_extended.price,2),
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.vatpercentage,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.type,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_types.isMain,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.updateCycle,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.showInPublic,
                                    ')#%',tbl_shop_products_extended.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_categories.category,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products.active,
                                    ')#%', IF(CHAR_LENGTH(tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription) > 0, tbl_shop_products_extended.longDescription, "")
                                    ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.id DESC
                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS productDetails
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_extended
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products_types ON tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId = tbl_shop_products_types.id
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products.id = tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_categories ON tbl_shop_categories.id = tbl_shop_products.categoryId

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productId
                            ORDER BY tbl_shop_products_extended.productTypeId DESC
                            
                        ) tblShopProductDetails ON `tblShopProductDetails`.`productTypeId` = `tbl_shop_products_types`.`id` AND `tblShopProductDetails`.`name` = `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`name`
LEFT JOIN (
                            SELECT 
                                tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                GROUP_CONCAT(
                                    tbl_shop_products_addons.productId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.addonProductId,
                                    ')#%', tbl_shop_products_addons.productExtendedId

                                    SEPARATOR ")$="                                    
                                ) AS addons
                            FROM
                                tbl_shop_products_addons
                            INNER JOIN
                                tbl_shop_products ON tbl_shop_products_addons.productId = tbl_shop_products.id

                            GROUP BY tbl_shop_products_addons.productId
                            
                        ) tblShopAddons ON `tblShopAddons`.`productId` = `tbl_shop_products`.`id`
WHERE `tbl_shop_categories`.`userId` = 1162
AND `tbl_shop_categories`.`active` = '1'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeFrom` <= '2020-07-27 16:10:59'
AND `tbl_shop_products`.`dateTimeTo` > '2020-07-27 16:10:59'
GROUP BY `tbl_shop_products_extended`.`productId`
ORDER BY `tbl_shop_categories`.`sortNumber`
